<Time>1551234065537< /Time><rate>4</rate>< Text>
My mother, Dorothy, (age 84) was sent by Kaiser to Roseville Care Center for extended care through Medicare and Medi-cal following a heart attack (CHF). While the decor is not the latest, they actually focus on what is important for the residents. The Care Center is clean, nice meals are cooked on site, the staff has empathy and always maintain the dignity of each resident. We were only there a short time and the last 5 days my mom was also under hospice care. The staff was very caring and my mom was moved to a private room; a cart was even brought in to our family with refreshments after seeing how many hours we were by my mom's side. We really appreciated the care and compassion shown to my mom and all of us from the Director of Nurses, RN's and CNA's.<//Text>

<name>Ilan<//name>< text>
My current 3-star rank is all about the brunch, dinner might be a better idea. Let's start with the bottom line first

The good
* Mimosas were great
* Quiche was very generous. Huge dishes overall

The bad
* Eggs Benedict - I usually complain that I'm given way too much Hollandaise sauce, in this case, it was almost non-existent, which made the whole thing very dry. Eggs were overcooked, and the potatoes on the side were most probably microwave re-heated or at least didn't feel fresh
* French toast was dry and very mediocre. I think this was the first time I didn't mind sharing one with others.
* Pizza - It's an Italian place, so we had high expectations - Very meh. Just a very mediocre, regular pizza. Nothing to write home about.
* Service - We were five people, with five different brunch orders and it took about 25-30 minutes until we got our order. We were not too hungry, so that was fine, but we did get to the point in the conversation when you begin to ask yourselves "where is our food" and look around.

It's an OK brunch, but with the high number of other, better brunches you have in the city, I would advise against getting one here.
The place itself is nice, and the crowd was older from I usually encounter in other locations. That's not a bad thing, of course, just an observation. While I might come back and try the dinner service, I won't be coming back for a brunch</text>

< Text>
A disappointing experience. My first time. I ordered the smoked trout and fettuccine. With Caesar salad. The salad was not a true Caesar. It was served with whole leaf romaine. Cheap cheese. Not the right blend of dressing ingredients.
The trout entree was a plate of fettuccine. I could barely find the trout, which was little flakes of overly smoked trout. I‚Äôm not sure it was trout because the smoked flavor was overwhelming and cancelled any sweetness or natural flavor of the trout. It was prepared with lemon, basil, and a green pepper. Again the peppers which were supposed to be mild was very hot and again overwhelmed any citrus or basil flavor.
Fettuccine was not fresh made.
They served Hawaiian roles instead of fresh baked bread.
I had the Cab Franc.  Again. A disappointing choice. I think it was old. It had a peculiar note that smelled like a chemical, not oak or berry.
Just a terribly high priced meal with the wrong combinations of flavor or compliment.
I do not recommend.
Nothing Italian about the meal-  maybe Mexican fettuccine.</Text>

< text>
When I initially decided I would like to have dental implants, I did a lot of on line research to educate myself about procedures, risks, and costs.  I found some clinics hyping great results at low prices.  These on line advertisements sounded too good to be true, so I steered clear of them.  I dug deeper and learned of patients who had suffered devastating jaw disfiguration subsequent to surgery performed by incompetent surgeons.

Fortunately, I also learned of Dr. Ash Vasanthan through diligent research.

Still with some trepidation, I entered Dr. Vasanthan‚Äôs suite for my first appointment, where I was greeted by friendly, professional staff, Cabrina and Sheri.

Dr. Vasanthan patiently detailed the procedures that I would need.  His explanations were accompanied by visual aids, which made the process easy to grasp.  Dr. Vasanthan also clearly explained risks involved with the procedures.  His patience and honesty, combined with his knowledge, kindness, and professional demeanor, convinced me that I had made the right choice coming to him.  It was also good to see that his staff thinks exceedingly well of him.

I am 100% happy with my dental implants, and wholeheartedly recommend Dr. Vasanthan, not only for his expertise and surgical skill, but also for his warm and thoughtful staff members, one and all, who go out of their way to make every visit a good experience as does he.  Special thanks to Cabrina and office manager Sheri.< /text>

<Time>1550347451026<//Time><Rating>3<//Rating><text>The pitch is 'High-class Steakhouse', but the delivery is slightly less.
The restaurant is located in a two story mini-mall in Encino. Parking is underneath & will cost you $5 to self-park. The room itself is small in comparison to typical steakhouses and lacks the leather booths you get at Musso, Ruth's Chris or practically all others. I was there a little after 6 on a Friday and it was packed already. I ordered the dry aged New York strip and, at $65, it wasn't as infused and flavorful as you'd expect, but it did have the nutty nuance dry ageing produces. It's not a rip-off, but expensive for the overall product. I asked for bread twice and never got it. Sides were tasty and generous.
Overall, the service is ok and the quality is good, but at $100 for a steak, two half sides and one drink, the price point is too high. Better steaks with better service are available elsewhere.</text><pics>None<//pics><Resp>None< /Resp>< gmapID>

<UserId.>100624082854812171481<//UserId.>< username>
Stephanie Chang< /username>
<date>1579900076692<//date><rate>5</rate>< text>
This is such a gem of a place! Don't let its small, side-of-the-road Lomita location fool you - there is great food here at great prices! Everything is fresh and tastes like a home-cooked meal. The bathrooms are clean and the staff is welcoming and friendly.

Breakfast is SO good here. Both the pancakes and french bread are fluffy and satisfying. The breakfast burrito is tasty and huge for a to-go option via the drive-thru window. No freezer burnt hash browns or soggy bacon!  Great selections for omelettes. My go-to is the spinach & feta omelette.

I mainly think of this as a favorite brunch place but I'd be wrong not to let everyone know about two other fantastic menu items here: the chili cheese fries and the chile verde.

The chili cheese fries = generous portion of delicious french fries topped with delicious beef chili and a generous topping of cheese. When I want a treat, I think of these chili cheese fries. It's a big cheat item for me but sooo worth it!

Chile Verde = I'm not generally a Mexican food aficionado. I can enjoy a nice plate of beans, rice and meat but it's not what I usually yearn for. However, I CRAVE the chile verde here. Somehow, the flavor and tenderness of the chile verde here has me hooked. I can't stop eating it and I can't stop wondering when I will eat it again!  I've stopped ordering chile verde at other places because I always get disappointed when it doesn't taste like Lomita's Best.

I really hope this place does not close down! They truly are doing a service to the community by providing a pleasant place to gather for a delicious, casual meal. Thank you, Lomita's Best!< /text>

<UserId.>106552469077367160003<//UserId.><username>Alan Ray<//username>< text>
I have been there twice this year so far...the restaurant and restrooms are a lot cleaner than most Mexican restaurants...that's a plus...I had the favorite according to the staff; of the bacon, avacodo, cheese burger. I ordered it to go and like I always do now, I ask for all the condiments on the side. I do that for two reasons, no soggy bun, I can pick & choose what looks good enough to put on the sandwich, and oh I guess there is a third reason, so I don't get a lettuce, onion & cheese only sandwich...and why are the onions served at "fast food" restaurants so damn "nasty"....
I know you waiting with bating breath for my order the second time...I dined in the outside patio with my Dog "Jack" and had the "T"-bone steak as they called it..with mashed potatoes and steamed vegetables...all was good except the steak had a lot to be desired, too thin like always in a small Mexican restaurant, but then again it was $11 and change so I guess I can't complain too much..my Dog had some bones to knaw on along with the hard parts I couldn't eat...I would go back and eat again, they are pretty efficient with the food.</text>

< text>
First off I would like to say that everyone I met at the center was very nice, (speakers and classmates). I took the 3 hour class where the speaker lectured to the students in regards to how to make money in the stock futures and options market. During the speech, I was called into a private room and was given a pressure sales pitch to purchase classes that was very expensive. I told the sales person that I could not afford them. The sales person said,  "let me see if you qualify for a loan." When the sales person came back, "I was told you are all set if you can come up with a specific amount." After speaking with other students in my 3 hour class, I found they got the same sales pitch and qualified for the same loan amount. I took the class twice at the center and took careful notes each time and I have also taken lots of the online classes XLT. I even tried using pro picks (the ticker symbols recommended daily by OTA for trading). Only to find out that the majority of trades stop out for a lost. The strategy does not work and to make matters even worse the center that I paid to attend in my area has shut down. The students that I have spoken with in my area have had the same experience. Please see attachment.Posted by Floyd H.< /text>

<rating>1< /rating><Review>Update 9/2/20. After my original review was posted, I received a call from Chris Crum, the owner of OTA KC. His voicemail said wanted to discuss my "request for a refund". I responded in writing, stating we needed written communication for both of our interest. No response after 3 weeks. Also, they disabled reviews on their Facebook page so that my review could not be seen there.

As a "Mastermind Student" (top package), I am 100% DISSATISFIED with OTA OF KC, and my "investment" into OTA has been a complete waste of time and money.
1. OTA OF KC Misrepresented the Time Investment Required
2. OTA OF KC Misrepresented Projected Income
3. OTA CORPORATE'S Training "Product" Contains Significant Amount of Conflicts in Training Instruction

1. OTA OF KC frequently cited the following before purchase: "You can set your trades and forget it. You only need a couple of hours each day. Trade anytime day or night. Most students are profitable within six months." The realities are that time investment required is substantial, and OTA trainers refuted these claims in more advanced classes from other areas that stated:
"Setting your trades and not monitoring them is a high risk for loss and not advised. Setting your trades at night and letting them run is foolish. It takes years, many hours of training, and tons of hard work to become a profitable trader. Technically you can place a trade any time of day, but doing so outside of the peak hours of 7 AM to 11 AM M-F is foolish." The few successful traders I have spoken to all have stated that it took 3-5 years to become profitable, after spending 20+ hours each week.  None of my OTA fellow students I have kept in touch with have become profitable after 20 months and substantial time investment. OTA OF KC had foreknowledge about my schedule limitations, yet never provided caution of time needed. Repeatedly, they assured me of flexibility and minimal time investment.

2. OTA OF KC projected income thru a customized "trade plan". Goals, objectives, and projections were all provided by OTA OF KC, based on their calculations. As described above, Schedule limitations were NOT taken into account when accessing "trading risks" within their plan. OTA OF KC failed to disclose "No Entry Trades" during income projections, success rates, or training. OTA's own student accessible "MYOTA" website shows their "Pro Picks" professional trade recommendations from December 27, 2018, till May 27, 2020, are as follows::
558 recommended trades
35 Closed for Break Even
50 Closed for Loss
59 Closed for Profit
414 never made an entry (74%)
No entry trades use margin and limit the number of trades you can place per day, thereby affecting your profitability. Despite "no entry trades," accounting for over 74%, OTA OF KC failed to disclose "no entries" during training, trade plan creation or projected income. This information is not common knowledge by a novice trader. When I asked for help, OTA OF KC and OTA corporate said to "watch more videos".

3. Training materials are not taught consistently between instructors, which causes SIGNIFICANT confusion to students. It is unnecessarily frustrating and leads to students' poor trading results. This problem is common knowledge among OTA staff and trainers.  Drastic and vast differences in training methods require an immeasurable amount of time for a new student to determine correctly. Making OTA's "training product" a disputable "benefit" over other far less expensive trading classes.

All items stated in this review are verifiable. A simple google search into FTC suit against OTA validates these statements and confirms OTA's long-standing practice of buying off bad reviews.

When I requested a refund, they denied it. OTA OF KC cited a three-day clause for "returns". No product this complex or this expensive is possible within that short time-frame. OTA OF KC never saught to resolve my complaints, provide solutions, or even apologize despite spending $48k with their organization. A huge regret that I hope others avoid.< /Review><Pics>None< /Pics><resp>None<//resp>< gmap_id>

And yet, it isn't until  going through OTA's program and classes that I REALLY perceive my financial freedom.

Without reservation I can say Online Trading Academy is the top school for trading, with the most intelligent core program, a very nice campus design, dynamic instructors.. which makes this absolutely the best investment in yourself.  Thank you to the support staff here as they have made me realize my full potential for wealth and legacy.   I  highly recommend this school.  I have (5) children and would trust any of them to attend this school - in fact, it's now part of their architectural, engineering, firefighter, writer, veterinarian education plan.

Shouts outs:  Andy Dominguez for believing in me and giving me the opportunity.  Darren Kimoto, for relating and inspiring me, Erika Carrillo, for the support and patience, Larry Jacobson, for the guidance and teaching style, and for showing me the 'right way'.  Here I thought l was good.... I'm looking forward to being great.< /Text>

< Review>
I first attended OTA as a newbie in August and over the first three days was floored by the mass of knowledge nestled in the folds of Irvine's metropolis- knowledge that many if not all of my peers knew nothing of. I was back again in September for the ProTrader class and once again  was impressed by the professional expertise of the instructors and staff, but also the down to earth amicability that warms the otherwise A/Ced building.
Just yesterday I finished the ForEx class and now my head is full of invaluable information regarding HOW and WHY the markets work as they do.
Being the fresh outta high-schooler that I am, it was a thought provoking experience to be seated for days at a time by people who are a good ten, twenty, even fifty years older than me! The classes taught at OTA are really for anyone of any age so long as they have the dedication, interest, and learnability to really take in the cascade of knowledge. Every instructor is different- they all have different styles of teaching and trading and they respect that each and every student is an individual with their own mind and their own 'Why'.
OTA gets five stars in my reckoning because in the collective 15 days I've spent in classes their, I've learned about as much in a full semester of *normal* school; for those of you that know Plato's allegory of the Cave, it's like that.< /Review>

<rate>5<//rate>< Review>
My 17-year-old son is very good with money.  He started selling my cookies and brownies at school when he was 12, unbeknownst to me, and continually saved the money in a drawer.  I discovered it when he was 15, asked him about the stack of cash, and realized that my boy had a really good head on his shoulders.  I wanted to encourage him to use his piggy-bank wisely and all of the future income that he will make, so I looked into different programs that would teach him about economics, the stock market, making money.  He and I went to several presentations offered by a variety of investment "schools" or money-making programs.  The one that we liked the most was OTA.  We felt that it had the most comprehensive program for us to start with.  We liked the idea of becoming MasterMind students and being part of a community of like-minded people who could encourage and mentor us for the rest of our lives - especially my teenage son.
We have attended several of OTA's week-long classes and have learned more than we had imagined.  The instructors are all very different: different personalities and different teaching styles, but their core strategies for trading and doing well in the markets are consistent and reliable as long as you don't deviate from their proven methods.  We don't want to recreate the wheel; we just want to benefit from its creation. The same with OTA: we want to be as successful as all of the teachers and mentors, who are very willing to share the stories of their success and their techniques.  So, we'll do what they teach us to do and become successful ourselves.
We are beginning to trade "live," after gaining some valuable practice from the simulated account.  The income potential is huge and we love being part of a global billion dollar industry that changes constantly. The freedom and flexibility that trading will provide for us is what I have been looking for for years. I'm leaving my 24-year legal career to do something really exciting and fun!  As for my son, he is going away to college in the fall.  People have asked us, "Why does he even need to go to school?  He's going to be really successful at trading!"  It's up to him what he wants to do -- and it's up to you to take charge of your life too.  This could be the key to your future.  I know it is for him, and it is for me.<//Review>

< Review>
Jim and the others are amazing. Now, during the pandemic, they are perfectly suited for the job. You wait in line outdoors---I've gone usually between 2 pm and 5 pm and there have never been more than 2 or 3 people ahead of me---order your fruit and veggies which are on display behind a roped off area. The attendant puts them in a basket and sets them aside. Then you use your phone to call the other attendant who's inside the store and order from the menu of items on a whiteboard you can peruse while waiting.  Items include very fresh fish and meats and cheeses.  Almost everything is made by local artisans...primarily in West Marin. They have fresh Ramini Mozzarella di bufala.  I've lived most of the last 30 years in Italy and this is the ONLY mozzarella I've found that tastes like mozzarella...buonissima.  From Edmund< /Review>

<Text>A gem of a resource for the community. Excellent, 100% organic farm produce, much of it truly local. The owner is a friendly man who cares a ton about what he sells. Prices are high compared to some other North Bay farm stands, but this is a wonderful alternative to driving down into the big town of Fairfax to shop at The Good Earth, if you don't feel like dealing with traffic and live in Lagunitas, Olema, Woodacre, Nicasio, etc.

Open year-round and well worth a visit. Adds to Marin's local food security in a very important way.</Text>< resp>
